<s> as his hansom debouched on to the embankment a man in top hat and overcoat passed walking quickly so close to the wall that he seemed to be scraping it <\s>
<s> thought jolyon soames himself <\s>
<s> what's he up to now <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab round the corner he got out and retraced his steps to where he could see the entrance to the mansions <\s>
<s> soames had halted in front of them and was looking up at the light in her windows <\s>
<s> if he goes in thought jolyon what shall i do <\s>
<s> what have i the right to do <\s>
<s> what the fellow had said was true <\s>
<s> she was still his wife absolutely without protection from annoyance <\s>
<s> well if he goes in he thought i follow <\s>
<s> and he began moving towards the mansions <\s>
<s> again soames advanced he was in the very entrance now <\s>
<s> but suddenly he stopped spun round on his heel and came back towards the river <\s>
<s> in a dozen steps he'll recognise me <\s>
<s> and he turned tail <\s>
<s> his cousin's footsteps kept pace with his own <\s>
<s> but he reached his cab and got in before soames had turned the corner <\s>
<s> he said through the trap <\s>
<s> soames figure ranged up alongside <\s>
<s> the quick suspicion on his cousin's face white in the lamplight decided him <\s>
<s> i can give you a lift he said if you're going west <\s>
<s> thanks answered soames and got in <\s>
<s> i've been seeing irene said jolyon when the cab had started <\s>
<s> you went to see her yesterday yourself i understand <\s>
<s> i did said soames she's my wife you know <\s>
<s> the tone the half lifted sneering lip roused sudden anger in jolyon but he subdued it <\s>
<s> you ought to know best he said but if you want a divorce it's not very wise to go seeing her is it <\s>
<s> one can't run with the hare and hunt with the hounds <\s>
<s> you're very good to warn me said soames but i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> she has said jolyon looking straight before him you can't take things up you know as they were twelve years ago <\s>
<s> that remains to be seen <\s>
<s> said jolyon she's in a damnable position and i am the only person with any legal say in her affairs <\s>
<s> except myself retorted soames who am also in a damnable position <\s>
<s> hers is what she made for herself mine what she made for me <\s>
<s> i am not at all sure that in her own interests i shan't require her to return to me <\s>
<s> exclaimed jolyon and a shiver went through his whole body <\s>
<s> i don't know what you may mean by what answered soames coldly your say in her affairs is confined to paying out her income please bear that in mind <\s>
<s> in choosing not to disgrace her by a divorce i retained my rights and as i say i am not at all sure that i shan't require to exercise them <\s>
<s> ejaculated jolyon and he uttered a short laugh <\s>
<s> yes said soames and there was a deadly quality in his voice <\s>
<s> i've not forgotten the nickname your father gave me the man of property <\s>
<s> i'm not called names for nothing <\s>
<s> this is fantastic murmured jolyon <\s>
<s> well the fellow couldn't force his wife to live with him <\s>
<s> those days were past anyway <\s>
<s> and he looked around at soames with the thought is he real this man <\s>
<s> but soames looked very real sitting square yet almost elegant with the clipped moustache on his pale face and a tooth showing where a lip was lifted in a fixed smile <\s>
<s> there was a long silence while jolyon thought instead of helping her i've made things worse <\s>
<s> suddenly soames said it would be the best thing that could happen to her in many ways <\s>
<s> at those words such a turmoil began taking place in jolyon that he could barely sit still in the cab <\s>
<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>
<s> here beside him in the cab was the very embodiment the corporeal sum as it were of the possessive instinct his own kinsman too <\s>
<s> it was uncanny and intolerable <\s>
<s> but there's something more in it than that <\s>
<s> he thought with a sick feeling <\s>
<s> the dog they say returns to his vomit <\s>
<s> the sight of her has reawakened something <\s>
<s> the devil's in it <\s>
<s> as i say said soames i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> i shall be obliged if you will kindly leave her quite alone <\s>
<s> jolyon bit his lips he who had always hated rows almost welcomed the thought of one now <\s>
<s> i can give you no such promise he said shortly <\s>
<s> very well said soames then we know where we are <\s>
<s> i'll get down here <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab he got out without word or sign of farewell <\s>
<s> jolyon travelled on to his club <\s>
<s> the first news of the war was being called in the streets but he paid no attention <\s>
<s> what could he do to help her <\s>
<s> if only his father were alive <\s>
<s> he could have done so much <\s>
<s> but why could he not do all that his father could have done <\s>
<s> was he not old enough turned fifty and twice married with grown up daughters and a son <\s>
<s> if she were plain i shouldn't be thinking twice about it <\s>
<s> beauty is the devil when you're sensitive to it <\s>
<s> and into the club reading room he went with a disturbed heart <\s>
<s> in that very room he and bosinney had talked one summer afternoon he well remembered even now the disguised and secret lecture he had given that young man in the interests of june the diagnosis of the forsytes he had hazarded and how he had wondered what sort of woman it was he was warning him against <\s>
<s> he was almost in want of a warning himself <\s>
<s> he thought really deuced funny <\s>
<s> chapter xiv soames discovers what he wants it is so much easier to say then we know where we are than to mean anything particular by the words <\s>
<s> and in saying them soames did but vent the jealous rankling of his instincts <\s>
<s> he got out of the cab in a state of wary anger with himself for not having seen irene with jolyon for having seen her and now with his inability to tell exactly what he wanted <\s>
<s> he had abandoned the cab because he could not bear to remain seated beside his cousin and walking briskly eastwards he thought i wouldn't trust that fellow jolyon a yard <\s>
<s> once outcast always outcast <\s>
<s> the chap had a natural sympathy with with laxity he had shied at the word sin because it was too melodramatic for use by a forsyte <\s>
<s> indecision in desire was to him a new feeling <\s>
<s> he was like a child between a promised toy and an old one which had been taken away from him and he was astonished at himself <\s>
<s> only last sunday desire had seemed simple just his freedom and annette <\s>
<s> i'll go and dine there he thought <\s>
<s> to see her might bring back his singleness of intention calm his exasperation clear his mind <\s>
<s> the restaurant was fairly full a good many foreigners and folk whom from their appearance he took to be literary or artistic <\s>
<s> scraps of conversation came his way through the clatter of plates and glasses <\s>
<s> he distinctly heard the boers sympathised with the british government blamed <\s>
<s> don't think much of their clientele he thought <\s>
<s> he went stolidly through his dinner and special coffee without making his presence known and when at last he had finished was careful not to be seen going towards the sanctum of madame lamotte <\s>
<s> they were as he entered having supper such a much nicer looking supper than the dinner he had eaten that he felt a kind of grief and they greeted him with a surprise so seemingly genuine that he thought with sudden suspicion i believe they knew i was here all the time <\s>

<s> hers is what she made for herself mine what she made for me <\s>
<s> i am not at all sure that in her own interests i shan't require her to return to me <\s>
<s> exclaimed jolyon and a shiver went through his whole body <\s>
<s> i don't know what you may mean by what answered soames coldly your say in her affairs is confined to paying out her income please bear that in mind <\s>

<s> suddenly soames said it would be the best thing that could happen to her in many ways <\s>

<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>

<s> only last sunday desire had seemed simple just his freedom and annette <\s>
<s> i'll go and dine there he thought <\s>
<s> to see her might bring back his singleness of intention calm his exasperation clear his mind <\s>
<s> the restaurant was fairly full a good many foreigners and folk whom from their appearance he took to be literary or artistic <\s>
<s> scraps of conversation came his way through the clatter of plates and glasses <\s>
<s> he distinctly heard the boers sympathised with the british government blamed <\s>
<s> don't think much of their clientele he thought <\s>
<s> he went stolidly through his dinner and special coffee without making his presence known and when at last he had finished was careful not to be seen going towards the sanctum of madame lamotte <\s>
<s> they were as he entered having supper such a much nicer looking supper than the dinner he had eaten that he felt a kind of grief and they greeted him with a surprise so seemingly genuine that he thought with sudden suspicion i believe they knew i was here all the time <\s>
<s> he gave annette a look furtive and searching <\s>
<s> so pretty seemingly so candid could she be angling for him <\s>
<s> he turned to madame lamotte and said i've been dining here <\s>
<s> if she had only known <\s>
<s> there were dishes she could have recommended what a pity <\s>
<s> as his hansom debouched on to the embankment a man in top hat and overcoat passed walking quickly so close to the wall that he seemed to be scraping it <\s>
<s> thought jolyon soames himself <\s>
<s> what's he up to now <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab round the corner he got out and retraced his steps to where he could see the entrance to the mansions <\s>
<s> soames had halted in front of them and was looking up at the light in her windows <\s>
<s> if he goes in thought jolyon what shall i do <\s>
<s> what have i the right to do <\s>
<s> what the fellow had said was true <\s>
<s> she was still his wife absolutely without protection from annoyance <\s>
<s> well if he goes in he thought i follow <\s>
<s> and he began moving towards the mansions <\s>
<s> again soames advanced he was in the very entrance now <\s>
<s> but suddenly he stopped spun round on his heel and came back towards the river <\s>
<s> in a dozen steps he'll recognise me <\s>
<s> and he turned tail <\s>
<s> his cousin's footsteps kept pace with his own <\s>
<s> but he reached his cab and got in before soames had turned the corner <\s>
<s> he said through the trap <\s>
<s> soames figure ranged up alongside <\s>
<s> the quick suspicion on his cousin's face white in the lamplight decided him <\s>
<s> i can give you a lift he said if you're going west <\s>
<s> thanks answered soames and got in <\s>
<s> i've been seeing irene said jolyon when the cab had started <\s>
<s> you went to see her yesterday yourself i understand <\s>
<s> i did said soames she's my wife you know <\s>
<s> the tone the half lifted sneering lip roused sudden anger in jolyon but he subdued it <\s>
<s> you ought to know best he said but if you want a divorce it's not very wise to go seeing her is it <\s>
<s> one can't run with the hare and hunt with the hounds <\s>
<s> you're very good to warn me said soames but i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> she has said jolyon looking straight before him you can't take things up you know as they were twelve years ago <\s>
<s> that remains to be seen <\s>
<s> said jolyon she's in a damnable position and i am the only person with any legal say in her affairs <\s>
<s> except myself retorted soames who am also in a damnable position <\s>
<s> hers is what she made for herself mine what she made for me <\s>
<s> i am not at all sure that in her own interests i shan't require her to return to me <\s>
<s> exclaimed jolyon and a shiver went through his whole body <\s>
<s> i don't know what you may mean by what answered soames coldly your say in her affairs is confined to paying out her income please bear that in mind <\s>
<s> in choosing not to disgrace her by a divorce i retained my rights and as i say i am not at all sure that i shan't require to exercise them <\s>
<s> ejaculated jolyon and he uttered a short laugh <\s>
<s> yes said soames and there was a deadly quality in his voice <\s>
<s> i've not forgotten the nickname your father gave me the man of property <\s>
<s> i'm not called names for nothing <\s>
<s> this is fantastic murmured jolyon <\s>
<s> well the fellow couldn't force his wife to live with him <\s>
<s> those days were past anyway <\s>
<s> and he looked around at soames with the thought is he real this man <\s>
<s> but soames looked very real sitting square yet almost elegant with the clipped moustache on his pale face and a tooth showing where a lip was lifted in a fixed smile <\s>
<s> there was a long silence while jolyon thought instead of helping her i've made things worse <\s>
<s> suddenly soames said it would be the best thing that could happen to her in many ways <\s>
<s> at those words such a turmoil began taking place in jolyon that he could barely sit still in the cab <\s>
<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>
<s> here beside him in the cab was the very embodiment the corporeal sum as it were of the possessive instinct his own kinsman too <\s>
<s> it was uncanny and intolerable <\s>
<s> but there's something more in it than that <\s>
<s> he thought with a sick feeling <\s>
<s> the dog they say returns to his vomit <\s>
<s> the sight of her has reawakened something <\s>
<s> the devil's in it <\s>
<s> as i say said soames i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> i shall be obliged if you will kindly leave her quite alone <\s>
<s> jolyon bit his lips he who had always hated rows almost welcomed the thought of one now <\s>
<s> i can give you no such promise he said shortly <\s>
<s> very well said soames then we know where we are <\s>
<s> i'll get down here <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab he got out without word or sign of farewell <\s>
<s> jolyon travelled on to his club <\s>

<s> beauty is the devil when you're sensitive to it <\s>

<s> thanks answered soames and got in <\s>

<s> i did said soames she's my wife you know <\s>
<s> the tone the half lifted sneering lip roused sudden anger in jolyon but he subdued it <\s>
<s> you ought to know best he said but if you want a divorce it's not very wise to go seeing her is it <\s>
<s> one can't run with the hare and hunt with the hounds <\s>
<s> you're very good to warn me said soames but i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> she has said jolyon looking straight before him you can't take things up you know as they were twelve years ago <\s>
<s> that remains to be seen <\s>
<s> said jolyon she's in a damnable position and i am the only person with any legal say in her affairs <\s>
<s> except myself retorted soames who am also in a damnable position <\s>
<s> hers is what she made for herself mine what she made for me <\s>
<s> i am not at all sure that in her own interests i shan't require her to return to me <\s>
<s> exclaimed jolyon and a shiver went through his whole body <\s>
<s> i don't know what you may mean by what answered soames coldly your say in her affairs is confined to paying out her income please bear that in mind <\s>
<s> in choosing not to disgrace her by a divorce i retained my rights and as i say i am not at all sure that i shan't require to exercise them <\s>
<s> ejaculated jolyon and he uttered a short laugh <\s>
<s> yes said soames and there was a deadly quality in his voice <\s>
<s> i've not forgotten the nickname your father gave me the man of property <\s>
<s> i'm not called names for nothing <\s>
<s> this is fantastic murmured jolyon <\s>
<s> well the fellow couldn't force his wife to live with him <\s>
<s> those days were past anyway <\s>
<s> and he looked around at soames with the thought is he real this man <\s>

<s> there was a long silence while jolyon thought instead of helping her i've made things worse <\s>
<s> suddenly soames said it would be the best thing that could happen to her in many ways <\s>
<s> at those words such a turmoil began taking place in jolyon that he could barely sit still in the cab <\s>
<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>
<s> here beside him in the cab was the very embodiment the corporeal sum as it were of the possessive instinct his own kinsman too <\s>
<s> it was uncanny and intolerable <\s>
<s> but there's something more in it than that <\s>
<s> he thought with a sick feeling <\s>
<s> the dog they say returns to his vomit <\s>
<s> the sight of her has reawakened something <\s>
<s> the devil's in it <\s>
<s> as i say said soames i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> i shall be obliged if you will kindly leave her quite alone <\s>

<s> so pretty seemingly so candid could she be angling for him <\s>

<s> there were dishes she could have recommended what a pity <\s>

<s> thought jolyon soames himself <\s>
<s> what's he up to now <\s>

<s> thanks answered soames and got in <\s>

<s> i did said soames she's my wife you know <\s>
<s> the tone the half lifted sneering lip roused sudden anger in jolyon but he subdued it <\s>
<s> you ought to know best he said but if you want a divorce it's not very wise to go seeing her is it <\s>
<s> one can't run with the hare and hunt with the hounds <\s>
<s> you're very good to warn me said soames but i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> she has said jolyon looking straight before him you can't take things up you know as they were twelve years ago <\s>
<s> that remains to be seen <\s>
<s> said jolyon she's in a damnable position and i am the only person with any legal say in her affairs <\s>
<s> except myself retorted soames who am also in a damnable position <\s>
<s> hers is what she made for herself mine what she made for me <\s>
<s> i am not at all sure that in her own interests i shan't require her to return to me <\s>
<s> exclaimed jolyon and a shiver went through his whole body <\s>
<s> i don't know what you may mean by what answered soames coldly your say in her affairs is confined to paying out her income please bear that in mind <\s>
<s> in choosing not to disgrace her by a divorce i retained my rights and as i say i am not at all sure that i shan't require to exercise them <\s>
<s> ejaculated jolyon and he uttered a short laugh <\s>
<s> yes said soames and there was a deadly quality in his voice <\s>

<s> i'm not called names for nothing <\s>

<s> and he looked around at soames with the thought is he real this man <\s>

<s> there was a long silence while jolyon thought instead of helping her i've made things worse <\s>
<s> suddenly soames said it would be the best thing that could happen to her in many ways <\s>
<s> at those words such a turmoil began taking place in jolyon that he could barely sit still in the cab <\s>
<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>
<s> here beside him in the cab was the very embodiment the corporeal sum as it were of the possessive instinct his own kinsman too <\s>

<s> the devil's in it <\s>

<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>

<s> and in saying them soames did but vent the jealous rankling of his instincts <\s>

<s> he had abandoned the cab because he could not bear to remain seated beside his cousin and walking briskly eastwards he thought i wouldn't trust that fellow jolyon a yard <\s>
<s> once outcast always outcast <\s>

<s> indecision in desire was to him a new feeling <\s>
<s> he was like a child between a promised toy and an old one which had been taken away from him and he was astonished at himself <\s>

<s> i'll go and dine there he thought <\s>
<s> to see her might bring back his singleness of intention calm his exasperation clear his mind <\s>
<s> the restaurant was fairly full a good many foreigners and folk whom from their appearance he took to be literary or artistic <\s>
<s> scraps of conversation came his way through the clatter of plates and glasses <\s>
<s> he distinctly heard the boers sympathised with the british government blamed <\s>
<s> don't think much of their clientele he thought <\s>
<s> he went stolidly through his dinner and special coffee without making his presence known and when at last he had finished was careful not to be seen going towards the sanctum of madame lamotte <\s>
<s> they were as he entered having supper such a much nicer looking supper than the dinner he had eaten that he felt a kind of grief and they greeted him with a surprise so seemingly genuine that he thought with sudden suspicion i believe they knew i was here all the time <\s>
<s> he gave annette a look furtive and searching <\s>
<s> so pretty seemingly so candid could she be angling for him <\s>

<s> i did said soames she's my wife you know <\s>
<s> the tone the half lifted sneering lip roused sudden anger in jolyon but he subdued it <\s>
<s> you ought to know best he said but if you want a divorce it's not very wise to go seeing her is it <\s>
<s> one can't run with the hare and hunt with the hounds <\s>
<s> you're very good to warn me said soames but i have not made up my mind <\s>

<s> that remains to be seen <\s>

<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>

<s> and stopping the cab round the corner he got out and retraced his steps to where he could see the entrance to the mansions <\s>
<s> soames had halted in front of them and was looking up at the light in her windows <\s>

<s> what have i the right to do <\s>
<s> what the fellow had said was true <\s>
<s> she was still his wife absolutely without protection from annoyance <\s>
<s> well if he goes in he thought i follow <\s>
<s> and he began moving towards the mansions <\s>
<s> again soames advanced he was in the very entrance now <\s>
<s> but suddenly he stopped spun round on his heel and came back towards the river <\s>
<s> in a dozen steps he'll recognise me <\s>
<s> and he turned tail <\s>
<s> his cousin's footsteps kept pace with his own <\s>
<s> but he reached his cab and got in before soames had turned the corner <\s>
<s> he said through the trap <\s>
<s> soames figure ranged up alongside <\s>
<s> the quick suspicion on his cousin's face white in the lamplight decided him <\s>
<s> i can give you a lift he said if you're going west <\s>
<s> thanks answered soames and got in <\s>
<s> i've been seeing irene said jolyon when the cab had started <\s>
<s> you went to see her yesterday yourself i understand <\s>
<s> i did said soames she's my wife you know <\s>
<s> the tone the half lifted sneering lip roused sudden anger in jolyon but he subdued it <\s>
<s> you ought to know best he said but if you want a divorce it's not very wise to go seeing her is it <\s>
<s> one can't run with the hare and hunt with the hounds <\s>
<s> you're very good to warn me said soames but i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> she has said jolyon looking straight before him you can't take things up you know as they were twelve years ago <\s>
<s> that remains to be seen <\s>
<s> said jolyon she's in a damnable position and i am the only person with any legal say in her affairs <\s>
<s> except myself retorted soames who am also in a damnable position <\s>
<s> hers is what she made for herself mine what she made for me <\s>
<s> i am not at all sure that in her own interests i shan't require her to return to me <\s>
<s> exclaimed jolyon and a shiver went through his whole body <\s>
<s> i don't know what you may mean by what answered soames coldly your say in her affairs is confined to paying out her income please bear that in mind <\s>
<s> in choosing not to disgrace her by a divorce i retained my rights and as i say i am not at all sure that i shan't require to exercise them <\s>
<s> ejaculated jolyon and he uttered a short laugh <\s>
<s> yes said soames and there was a deadly quality in his voice <\s>
<s> i've not forgotten the nickname your father gave me the man of property <\s>
<s> i'm not called names for nothing <\s>
<s> this is fantastic murmured jolyon <\s>
<s> well the fellow couldn't force his wife to live with him <\s>
<s> those days were past anyway <\s>
<s> and he looked around at soames with the thought is he real this man <\s>
<s> but soames looked very real sitting square yet almost elegant with the clipped moustache on his pale face and a tooth showing where a lip was lifted in a fixed smile <\s>
<s> there was a long silence while jolyon thought instead of helping her i've made things worse <\s>
<s> suddenly soames said it would be the best thing that could happen to her in many ways <\s>
<s> at those words such a turmoil began taking place in jolyon that he could barely sit still in the cab <\s>
<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>
<s> here beside him in the cab was the very embodiment the corporeal sum as it were of the possessive instinct his own kinsman too <\s>
<s> it was uncanny and intolerable <\s>
<s> but there's something more in it than that <\s>
<s> he thought with a sick feeling <\s>
<s> the dog they say returns to his vomit <\s>
<s> the sight of her has reawakened something <\s>
<s> the devil's in it <\s>
<s> as i say said soames i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> i shall be obliged if you will kindly leave her quite alone <\s>
<s> jolyon bit his lips he who had always hated rows almost welcomed the thought of one now <\s>
<s> i can give you no such promise he said shortly <\s>
<s> very well said soames then we know where we are <\s>
<s> i'll get down here <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab he got out without word or sign of farewell <\s>
<s> jolyon travelled on to his club <\s>
<s> the first news of the war was being called in the streets but he paid no attention <\s>

<s> if she were plain i shouldn't be thinking twice about it <\s>
<s> beauty is the devil when you're sensitive to it <\s>
<s> and into the club reading room he went with a disturbed heart <\s>
<s> in that very room he and bosinney had talked one summer afternoon he well remembered even now the disguised and secret lecture he had given that young man in the interests of june the diagnosis of the forsytes he had hazarded and how he had wondered what sort of woman it was he was warning him against <\s>
<s> he was almost in want of a warning himself <\s>

<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>

<s> to see her might bring back his singleness of intention calm his exasperation clear his mind <\s>
<s> the restaurant was fairly full a good many foreigners and folk whom from their appearance he took to be literary or artistic <\s>
<s> scraps of conversation came his way through the clatter of plates and glasses <\s>
<s> he distinctly heard the boers sympathised with the british government blamed <\s>
<s> don't think much of their clientele he thought <\s>
<s> he went stolidly through his dinner and special coffee without making his presence known and when at last he had finished was careful not to be seen going towards the sanctum of madame lamotte <\s>
<s> they were as he entered having supper such a much nicer looking supper than the dinner he had eaten that he felt a kind of grief and they greeted him with a surprise so seemingly genuine that he thought with sudden suspicion i believe they knew i was here all the time <\s>
<s> he gave annette a look furtive and searching <\s>
<s> so pretty seemingly so candid could she be angling for him <\s>
<s> he turned to madame lamotte and said i've been dining here <\s>
<s> if she had only known <\s>
<s> there were dishes she could have recommended what a pity <\s>
<s> as his hansom debouched on to the embankment a man in top hat and overcoat passed walking quickly so close to the wall that he seemed to be scraping it <\s>
<s> thought jolyon soames himself <\s>
<s> what's he up to now <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab round the corner he got out and retraced his steps to where he could see the entrance to the mansions <\s>
<s> soames had halted in front of them and was looking up at the light in her windows <\s>
<s> if he goes in thought jolyon what shall i do <\s>
<s> what have i the right to do <\s>
<s> what the fellow had said was true <\s>
<s> she was still his wife absolutely without protection from annoyance <\s>
<s> well if he goes in he thought i follow <\s>
<s> and he began moving towards the mansions <\s>
<s> again soames advanced he was in the very entrance now <\s>
<s> but suddenly he stopped spun round on his heel and came back towards the river <\s>
<s> in a dozen steps he'll recognise me <\s>
<s> and he turned tail <\s>
<s> his cousin's footsteps kept pace with his own <\s>
<s> but he reached his cab and got in before soames had turned the corner <\s>
<s> he said through the trap <\s>
<s> soames figure ranged up alongside <\s>
<s> the quick suspicion on his cousin's face white in the lamplight decided him <\s>
<s> i can give you a lift he said if you're going west <\s>
<s> thanks answered soames and got in <\s>
<s> i've been seeing irene said jolyon when the cab had started <\s>
<s> you went to see her yesterday yourself i understand <\s>
<s> i did said soames she's my wife you know <\s>
<s> the tone the half lifted sneering lip roused sudden anger in jolyon but he subdued it <\s>
<s> you ought to know best he said but if you want a divorce it's not very wise to go seeing her is it <\s>
<s> one can't run with the hare and hunt with the hounds <\s>
<s> you're very good to warn me said soames but i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> she has said jolyon looking straight before him you can't take things up you know as they were twelve years ago <\s>
<s> that remains to be seen <\s>
<s> said jolyon she's in a damnable position and i am the only person with any legal say in her affairs <\s>
<s> except myself retorted soames who am also in a damnable position <\s>
<s> hers is what she made for herself mine what she made for me <\s>
<s> i am not at all sure that in her own interests i shan't require her to return to me <\s>
<s> exclaimed jolyon and a shiver went through his whole body <\s>
<s> i don't know what you may mean by what answered soames coldly your say in her affairs is confined to paying out her income please bear that in mind <\s>
<s> in choosing not to disgrace her by a divorce i retained my rights and as i say i am not at all sure that i shan't require to exercise them <\s>
<s> ejaculated jolyon and he uttered a short laugh <\s>
<s> yes said soames and there was a deadly quality in his voice <\s>
<s> i've not forgotten the nickname your father gave me the man of property <\s>
<s> i'm not called names for nothing <\s>
<s> this is fantastic murmured jolyon <\s>
<s> well the fellow couldn't force his wife to live with him <\s>
<s> those days were past anyway <\s>
<s> and he looked around at soames with the thought is he real this man <\s>
<s> but soames looked very real sitting square yet almost elegant with the clipped moustache on his pale face and a tooth showing where a lip was lifted in a fixed smile <\s>
<s> there was a long silence while jolyon thought instead of helping her i've made things worse <\s>
<s> suddenly soames said it would be the best thing that could happen to her in many ways <\s>
<s> at those words such a turmoil began taking place in jolyon that he could barely sit still in the cab <\s>
<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>
<s> here beside him in the cab was the very embodiment the corporeal sum as it were of the possessive instinct his own kinsman too <\s>
<s> it was uncanny and intolerable <\s>
<s> but there's something more in it than that <\s>
<s> he thought with a sick feeling <\s>
<s> the dog they say returns to his vomit <\s>
<s> the sight of her has reawakened something <\s>
<s> the devil's in it <\s>
<s> as i say said soames i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> i shall be obliged if you will kindly leave her quite alone <\s>
<s> jolyon bit his lips he who had always hated rows almost welcomed the thought of one now <\s>
<s> i can give you no such promise he said shortly <\s>
<s> very well said soames then we know where we are <\s>
<s> i'll get down here <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab he got out without word or sign of farewell <\s>
<s> jolyon travelled on to his club <\s>
<s> the first news of the war was being called in the streets but he paid no attention <\s>

<s> if she were plain i shouldn't be thinking twice about it <\s>
<s> beauty is the devil when you're sensitive to it <\s>
<s> and into the club reading room he went with a disturbed heart <\s>

<s> he was almost in want of a warning himself <\s>

<s> he said through the trap <\s>
<s> soames figure ranged up alongside <\s>
<s> the quick suspicion on his cousin's face white in the lamplight decided him <\s>
<s> i can give you a lift he said if you're going west <\s>
<s> thanks answered soames and got in <\s>
<s> i've been seeing irene said jolyon when the cab had started <\s>
<s> you went to see her yesterday yourself i understand <\s>
<s> i did said soames she's my wife you know <\s>
<s> the tone the half lifted sneering lip roused sudden anger in jolyon but he subdued it <\s>
<s> you ought to know best he said but if you want a divorce it's not very wise to go seeing her is it <\s>
<s> one can't run with the hare and hunt with the hounds <\s>
<s> you're very good to warn me said soames but i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> she has said jolyon looking straight before him you can't take things up you know as they were twelve years ago <\s>
<s> that remains to be seen <\s>
<s> said jolyon she's in a damnable position and i am the only person with any legal say in her affairs <\s>
<s> except myself retorted soames who am also in a damnable position <\s>
<s> hers is what she made for herself mine what she made for me <\s>
<s> i am not at all sure that in her own interests i shan't require her to return to me <\s>
<s> exclaimed jolyon and a shiver went through his whole body <\s>
<s> i don't know what you may mean by what answered soames coldly your say in her affairs is confined to paying out her income please bear that in mind <\s>
<s> in choosing not to disgrace her by a divorce i retained my rights and as i say i am not at all sure that i shan't require to exercise them <\s>
<s> ejaculated jolyon and he uttered a short laugh <\s>
<s> yes said soames and there was a deadly quality in his voice <\s>
<s> i've not forgotten the nickname your father gave me the man of property <\s>
<s> i'm not called names for nothing <\s>
<s> this is fantastic murmured jolyon <\s>
<s> well the fellow couldn't force his wife to live with him <\s>
<s> those days were past anyway <\s>
<s> and he looked around at soames with the thought is he real this man <\s>
<s> but soames looked very real sitting square yet almost elegant with the clipped moustache on his pale face and a tooth showing where a lip was lifted in a fixed smile <\s>
<s> there was a long silence while jolyon thought instead of helping her i've made things worse <\s>
<s> suddenly soames said it would be the best thing that could happen to her in many ways <\s>
<s> at those words such a turmoil began taking place in jolyon that he could barely sit still in the cab <\s>
<s> it was as if he were boxed up with hundreds of thousands of his countrymen boxed up with that something in the national character which had always been to him revolting something which he knew to be extremely natural and yet which seemed to him inexplicable their intense belief in contracts and vested rights their complacent sense of virtue in the exaction of those rights <\s>
<s> here beside him in the cab was the very embodiment the corporeal sum as it were of the possessive instinct his own kinsman too <\s>
<s> it was uncanny and intolerable <\s>
<s> but there's something more in it than that <\s>
<s> he thought with a sick feeling <\s>
<s> the dog they say returns to his vomit <\s>
<s> the sight of her has reawakened something <\s>
<s> the devil's in it <\s>
<s> as i say said soames i have not made up my mind <\s>
<s> i shall be obliged if you will kindly leave her quite alone <\s>
<s> jolyon bit his lips he who had always hated rows almost welcomed the thought of one now <\s>
<s> i can give you no such promise he said shortly <\s>
<s> very well said soames then we know where we are <\s>
<s> i'll get down here <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab he got out without word or sign of farewell <\s>
<s> jolyon travelled on to his club <\s>
<s> the first news of the war was being called in the streets but he paid no attention <\s>
<s> what could he do to help her <\s>
<s> if only his father were alive <\s>
<s> he could have done so much <\s>
<s> but why could he not do all that his father could have done <\s>
<s> was he not old enough turned fifty and twice married with grown up daughters and a son <\s>
<s> if she were plain i shouldn't be thinking twice about it <\s>
<s> beauty is the devil when you're sensitive to it <\s>
<s> and into the club reading room he went with a disturbed heart <\s>
<s> in that very room he and bosinney had talked one summer afternoon he well remembered even now the disguised and secret lecture he had given that young man in the interests of june the diagnosis of the forsytes he had hazarded and how he had wondered what sort of woman it was he was warning him against <\s>
<s> he was almost in want of a warning himself <\s>
<s> he thought really deuced funny <\s>
<s> chapter xiv soames discovers what he wants it is so much easier to say then we know where we are than to mean anything particular by the words <\s>
<s> and in saying them soames did but vent the jealous rankling of his instincts <\s>
<s> he got out of the cab in a state of wary anger with himself for not having seen irene with jolyon for having seen her and now with his inability to tell exactly what he wanted <\s>
<s> he had abandoned the cab because he could not bear to remain seated beside his cousin and walking briskly eastwards he thought i wouldn't trust that fellow jolyon a yard <\s>
<s> once outcast always outcast <\s>
<s> the chap had a natural sympathy with with laxity he had shied at the word sin because it was too melodramatic for use by a forsyte <\s>
<s> indecision in desire was to him a new feeling <\s>
<s> he was like a child between a promised toy and an old one which had been taken away from him and he was astonished at himself <\s>
<s> only last sunday desire had seemed simple just his freedom and annette <\s>
<s> i'll go and dine there he thought <\s>
<s> to see her might bring back his singleness of intention calm his exasperation clear his mind <\s>
<s> the restaurant was fairly full a good many foreigners and folk whom from their appearance he took to be literary or artistic <\s>
<s> scraps of conversation came his way through the clatter of plates and glasses <\s>
<s> he distinctly heard the boers sympathised with the british government blamed <\s>
<s> don't think much of their clientele he thought <\s>
<s> he went stolidly through his dinner and special coffee without making his presence known and when at last he had finished was careful not to be seen going towards the sanctum of madame lamotte <\s>
<s> they were as he entered having supper such a much nicer looking supper than the dinner he had eaten that he felt a kind of grief and they greeted him with a surprise so seemingly genuine that he thought with sudden suspicion i believe they knew i was here all the time <\s>
<s> he gave annette a look furtive and searching <\s>
<s> so pretty seemingly so candid could she be angling for him <\s>
<s> he turned to madame lamotte and said i've been dining here <\s>
<s> if she had only known <\s>
<s> there were dishes she could have recommended what a pity <\s>
<s> as his hansom debouched on to the embankment a man in top hat and overcoat passed walking quickly so close to the wall that he seemed to be scraping it <\s>
<s> thought jolyon soames himself <\s>
<s> what's he up to now <\s>
<s> and stopping the cab round the corner he got out and retraced his steps to where he could see the entrance to the mansions <\s>
<s> soames had halted in front of them and was looking up at the light in her windows <\s>
<s> if he goes in thought jolyon what shall i do <\s>
<s> what have i the right to do <\s>
<s> what the fellow had said was true <\s>
<s> she was still his wife absolutely without protection from annoyance <\s>
<s> well if he goes in he thought i follow <\s>
<s> and he began moving towards the mansions <\s>
<s> again soames advanced he was in the very entrance now <\s>
